    if (!shc.isBOT) {
  (function() {
    window.eventbt = new CustomEvent('btready');
    function push_bt() {
      console.log('analytics - signalDataReady');
      bt = $.extend(bt, {
        siteId: shc.chronStoreName.replace('-','').replace('us', 'com'),
        gaSite: shc.gaSite,
        pageType: bt.pageType || shc.getPageType(),
        isKiosk: shc.isKiosk
      });
      if (shc.gaSite.indexOf('none') < 0) {
          $(document).trigger('shc_et', ['pv', bt]);
          document.querySelector('body').dispatchEvent(eventbt);
      }
      if(typeof _satellite !== "undefined"){
            _satellite.track('dataLayerSet');
      }
    }
    
    if (window.SHC && $.q('body').attr('id') === 'browse-page') {
      //HACK: handle the new PDP bundle pages which have invalid body ID and don't trigger signalDataReady
      bt = $.extend(bt, {pageType: 'product', bundle:true});
      document.querySelector('body').dispatchEvent(eventbt); 
      push_bt();
    }
    else {
      $(document).on(shcWidgets.EVENTS.signalDataReady, push_bt);
      document.querySelector('body').dispatchEvent(eventbt);
    }
  }());
}

   <script>
    /* 24/7 Chat start */
if (shc.features.chat247) {
  shc.chat = {
    pageDetails: {
     pxpath: shc.env === 'PROD' ? 'PROD' : 'STAGE',
     international: !!shc.features.international,
     language: 'US',
     isPR: !!(shc.features.searsPR || shc.features.kmartPR),
     pageName: $('body').attr('id') || 'none',
     productVertical: window.omVrt || '',
     productCategory: window.omCat || '',
     productSubCategory: window.omSubCat || ''
   },
   EVENT: {pageLoad:'pageload', click: 'click'},
   SCOPE: {page: 'page', visitor: 'visitor'},
   send: function(scope, key, data, event) {
     if (window._tfsq === undefined) {
       window._tfsq = [];
     }
     _tfsq.push([scope, key, data, event]);
   }
  };

  if ($('body').attr('id') === 'product') {
    $(document).on(shcWidgets.EVENTS.chatDataReady, function(e, data) {
      if (data.data) {
        $.extend(shc.chat.pageDetails, data.data);
      }
      if ($('body').hasClass('ie8')) {shc.features.chat247=false;}
      var ch = shc.chat;
      //defer setting this b/c it's dependant on header getting all profile info
      ch.pageDetails.loginFlag = $('#profileArea.loggedIn').length > 0;
      ch.send(ch.SCOPE.page, 'pageDetails', ch.pageDetails, ch.EVENT.pageLoad);
    });
  }
  else {
    $(window).on('load', function() {
      if ($('body').hasClass('ie8')) {shc.features.chat247=false;}
      var ch = shc.chat;
      //defer setting this b/c it's dependant on header getting all profile info
      ch.pageDetails.loginFlag = $('#profileArea.loggedIn').length > 0;
      ch.send(ch.SCOPE.page, 'pageDetails', ch.pageDetails, ch.EVENT.pageLoad);
    });
  }
}
/* 24/7 Chat end */
   </script>

  <script type="text/javascript">
   if(screenWidth > 767) {
    window.bt = {
        "levelIds": "",
        "levels": "",
        "verticalId": "",
        "verticalName": "",
        "categoryID": "",
        "categoryName": "",
        "subCategoryID": "",
        "subCategoryName": "",
        "itemNumber": "",
        "beanType": "",
        "itemPrice": "N/A",
        "itemDiscount": "N/A",
        "productDescription": "",
        "oasSitePage": ""
    };
    (function() {
        var catArray = shc.catArray;
        var catIdArray = shc.catIdArray;
        if (catArray.length > 0) {
            var i = 0,
                l = Math.min(3, catArray.length);
            for (i = 0; i < l; i++) {
                switch (i) {
                    case 0:
                        bt.verticalName = catArray[i];
                        bt.levels = bt.verticalName;
                        bt.verticalId = catIdArray[i];
                        bt.levelIds = bt.verticalId;
                        break;
                    case 1:
                        bt.categoryName = catArray[i];
                        bt.levels += '_' + bt.categoryName;
                        bt.categoryID = catIdArray[i];
                        if (bt.categoryID !== "") {
                            bt.levelIds += '_' + bt.categoryID;
                        }
                        break;
                    case 2:
                        bt.subCategoryName = catArray[i];
                        bt.levels += '_' + bt.subCategoryName;
                        bt.subCategoryID = catIdArray[i];
                        if (bt.subCategoryID !== "") {
                            bt.levelIds += '_' + bt.subCategoryID;
                        }
                }
            }
        }
    })();
  
    $(document).trigger(shcWidgets.EVENTS.signalDataReady, { id: "homepage", data: window.bt });
}
 window.dispatchEvent(new Event("mobileaemevent"));
  </script>
